mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">填写律师不太积极主动填写问卷。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原来笔者计划回收问卷的数量是</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">200</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">份左右，笔者也由于从事法律行业，认识不少执业律师，但问卷发放给执业律师后，他们由于工作忙碌等原因，时常忘记打印、携带问卷进行填写。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">笔者至少联系过</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">100</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">位的律师进行问卷的填写，但实际上填写了问卷的律师只有</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">30</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">位左右。笔者需每隔两周进行提醒和催促，才有现在</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">101</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">份的样本问卷回收。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">其中新疆的律师告诉我</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，新疆特殊又特殊的区域，随时可能被教育，在会见过程中已经询问过被羁押人，其不愿意填问卷的内容。</span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0cm; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt; text-indent: 0cm;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="ZH-TW" style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">二、</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="background: white; color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">问卷的设计是主观问题多点好，还是客观问题多点好。<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大多数是客观问题，涉及主观性问题（拥挤程度、空气流通等），可根据律师在沟通过程中尽量问询，根据反馈情况填写。调查问题当中，定性分析是好做的，定量分析却需要更多的耐心和时间。</span><span style="background-color: white; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; margin-left: 0cm; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt; text-indent: 0cm;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="ZH-TW" style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">三、</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="background: white; color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">问卷的填写过程中出现的问题<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">问卷发放给执业律师后，执业律师填写中经常出现</span><b><i><u><span style="background: #D9D9D9; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">漏填</span></u></i></b><span style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">的情况，尤其是关于卫生间与张贴公示这两个问题，导致很多的选项无效，无法纳入调研统计的表格中。<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">自己分析为何会有如此多的漏填的情况发生，很大的原因在于问卷的内容有点过多。律师不熟悉问卷内容的话，填写整个问卷消耗的时间可能会至半个小时。导致很多律师其实就略过了很多问题，尤其明显的是最后四道文字题，百分之六十的律师一个字都没有填写。</span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">101</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">份回收调查表中，</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">涉及省会和直辖市的有</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">32</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">份问卷，涉及非省会和直辖市的有</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">69</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">份问卷。</span></p></span><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WwrK0TPyEdE/YBE-PItT-wI/AAAAAAABuEg/MFZgDDhQ5bk5pruAdcbtpLLCRYgXIv24ACLcBGAsYHQ/s710/2.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="550" data-original-width="710" height="310" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WwrK0TPyEdE/YBE-PItT-wI/AAAAAAABuEg/MFZgDDhQ5bk5pruAdcbtpLLCRYgXIv24ACLcBGAsYHQ/w400-h310/2.png" width="400" /></a><span style="background-color: #f8f8f8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt; text-align: left;">&nbsp;</span></div> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">问卷中被羁押人男女比例为</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">71</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">29</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（有一份问卷是律师根据看守所情况总结填写而成）</span></p><p></p><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-sgKHeYnBroc/YBE-m3FlPwI/AAAAAAABuEo/KDqkgnyBWYE1sqbNQhDAz4uSp94JQRwlgCLcBGAsYHQ/s592/3.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">完全不拥挤，个人活动空间很大，晚上睡觉可以有双人床大空间。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">）非常拥挤，晚上睡觉都是胸贴背侧着睡。</span><span style="background-color: #f8f8f8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">关于<b><u>仓内的空间</u></b></span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">【</span><span style="background: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《看守所建设标准》建标<b><span lang="ZH-TW">[2013]126</span></b>号第二十九条 看守所监室设计应符合下列要求：一、看守所监室分为普通监室和单人监室，并分别设置与之毗邻的室外活动场。普通监室每间关押人数应为<span lang="ZH-TW">8</span>～<span lang="ZH-TW">16</span>人，人均使用面积<span lang="ZH-TW">8</span>人监室宜为<span lang="ZH-TW">7m<sup>2</sup></span>，<span lang="ZH-TW">9</span>～<span lang="ZH-TW">16</span>人监室宜为<span lang="ZH-TW">5m<sup>2</sup></span>；单人监室每间使用面积宜为<span lang="ZH-TW">7</span>～<span lang="ZH-TW">8m<sup>2</sup></span>，每<span lang="ZH-TW">100</span>人设置<span lang="ZH-TW">1</span>～<span lang="ZH-TW">3</span>间。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: #666666; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">】</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><b><u><span style="background: #F8F8F8; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">有没有符合上述规定。</span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: red; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">但是鉴于每个当事人的文化水平不高，形容能力不强，所以选项里加了空间拥挤程</span><span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; font-size: 12pt;">）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">天气状况允许的情况下，你每日<b><u>室外活动时间</u></b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">有多少？</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="font-family: 宋体; &nbsp;</span><span style="background: rgb(248, 248, 248); font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;">（</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: rgb(248, 248, 248); font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">号）规定：</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">安排在押人员在中午和晚上休息时段双人值班，并每日滚动轮换</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="background: #F8F8F8; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-themecolor: text1;">;</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">告知值班人员发现异常立即报告，对有安全危险的在押人员不得安排值班</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">但事实上值夜班中断夜间的睡眠，很多在押人员在值夜班返回睡觉会感觉睡眠质量不高，影响休息。</span></p><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eQ2dnXEfM2o/YBFEevbCTsI/AAAAAAABuF8/mzeMTqfxFGgPiH-uS0NUykx3K-PE7kAmQCLcBGAsYHQ/s814/10.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: #484848; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">)</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">关于个人卫生之规则要求，</span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体_GB2312; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">规则</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体_GB2312; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女性囚犯的囚所应具备满足妇女特殊卫生需要所要求的设施和物品，包括</span><span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">免费提供卫生巾和正常供水以供儿童和妇女个人护理之用</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，尤其是对烹制食品的妇女和怀孕、哺乳或者例假时的妇女。</span><span lang="ZH-TW" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">】</span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly;"><b><span style="background: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">关于在押人员权利和义务</span></b><span style="background-color: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="1" style="line-height: 14.0pt; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-line-height-rule: exactly;"><span style="background: #F8F8F8; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">设计问题：</span><span style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">看守所有没有用书面的形式告之你的<b><u>在押人员权利和义务规定</u></b>？书面告知内容应有一份你收存。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-language: AR; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="1" style="line-height: 14.0pt; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-line-height-rule: exactly;"><span style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-language: AR; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">（<span lang="EN-US">A</span>）有书面告知，我有收存一份书面（<span lang="EN-US">B</span>）有书面告知，只给我看，没有给我书面。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="1" style="mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly;"><span style="background: white; color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-language: AR; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">（<span lang="EN-US">C</span>）只是口头告知（<span lang="EN-US">D</span>）没有任何形式告知过的</span><span style="background-color: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p> <p class="1" style="mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly;"><span style="background: white; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">【根据《看守所告知在押人员权利和义务的规定》：二、</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-bidi-language: AR; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">告知应当采取书面方式，告知书一式两联，一联交在押人员收存，一联由在押人员注明告知时间并签名、捺印后存入其档案。】</span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">考察有没有符合上述规定。</span></p><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-p-xXLf97IZ4/YBFMqtSVbMI/AAAAAAABuIY/IFFxBwpCdTkUAuL07IETm4yC1M3ebMdygCLcBGAsYHQ/s812/30.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">除了单项选择的问题外，还有三道主观问题调查。<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">关于残障部分<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 12.0pt; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-themecolor: text1;">设计问题：</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-themecolor: text1;">在监室里有没有见过<b><u>残障被羁押人</u></b>？<b><u><span style="background: white;">如见过回答此问题</span></u></b><span style="background: white;">，</span>比如肢体障碍，听力、语言障碍，视力障碍，甚至是智力、精神障碍的。如有，他们的待遇如何？会否因为无法听到、理解或执行管教的命令而受罚？有没有适合于肢体障碍的无障碍设施，比如扶手？<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; padding-right: 0cm; padding-top: 0cm;" valign="top">  <p style="line-height: 20.0pt; margin-left: 0cm; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; text-indent: 0cm;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">1、</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">看以所应当对成年人和未成年人实行分别关押和管理；对患有传染病处于传染期的在押人员，应当隔离关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>  <p style="line-height: 20.0pt; margin-left: 0cm; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; text-indent: 0cm;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span lang="EN-US" style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">2、</span></span><!--[endif]--><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年老、体弱、生病、残疾的在押人员与一般的在押人员一起进行关押，没有设置老弱病残监室。<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><b>为什么想要做关于看守所被羁押人待遇情况的调查报告？</b><span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">当我向别人介绍自己有这个报告的写作意愿时，这是向我问得最多的一个问题。</span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">最主要的原因看守所的生活状况在整个的国家系统里，像是一个神秘的存在，没有进去过的人，都不了解里面的状况如何。<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">每当我去看守所会见，很多家属很关心自己的亲属在看守所的生活状况好不好，会问我很多很多的问题。我也会逐一解答。<span lang="ZH-TW"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">所以我自己就在想，何不做一个关于全国看守所的一个随机调查？让公众也知道一下看守所一个大概全貌是什么。</span><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷宋 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">基于这样一个简单的想法，就做起来了。</span><span style="color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p><p class="a" style="line-height: 150%; mso-element-wrap: auto; mso-element: frame; mso-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 36.0pt 72.0pt 108.0pt 144.0pt 180.0pt 216.0pt 252.0pt 288.0pt 324.0pt 360.0pt 396.0pt 426.0pt;"><span style="background: white; color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;儷黑 Pro&quot;; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">对于帮助填写每一份问卷的律师，十分感谢各位无偿的帮助，我很清楚，每一份问卷都是律师们牺牲一部分会见时间回馈的，虽然这份报告</span><span style="background: #F8F8F8; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我也很清楚有不少瑕疵问题（请抱歉只有我一个人做这个设计与分析），</span><span style="background: white; color: red; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;
